<script type="text/javascript">
  (function(){
    const convertLang = (locale) => {
      let t = locale.toUpperCase();
      return "PT-BR" === t || "PT-PT" === t || "ZH-CN" === t || "ZH-TW" === t ? t.replace("-", "_") : t.match(/^[a-zA-Z]{2}-[a-zA-Z]{2}$/) ? t.substring(0, 2) : t
    }

    const sg_addon_setGlobalVariables = () => {
      try{
        let locale = "en";
        window["sg_addon_currentLanguage"] = convertLang(locale);
        window["sg_addon_defaultLanguage"] ="en";
        window["sg_addon_defaultRootUrl"] ="/";
        window["sg_addon_currentRootUrl"] ="/";
        window["sg_addon_shopLocales"] = sgAddonGetAllLocales();
      }catch(err){
        console.log("Language Config:- ",err);
      }
    }

    const sgAddonGetAllLocales = () => {
      let shopLocales = {};
      try{shopLocales["en"] = {
            endonymName : "English",
            isoCode : "en",
            name : "English",
            primary : true,
            rootUrl : "\/"
          };}catch(err){
        console.log("getAllLocales Config:- ",err);
      }
      return shopLocales;
    }

    sg_addon_setGlobalVariables();
    
    window["sg_addon_sfApiVersion"]='2024-01';
    window["sgAddon_moneyFormats"] = {
      "money": "Rs.{{amount}}",
      "moneyCurrency": "Rs.{{amount}} PKR"
    };
    window["sg_addon_groupsData"] = {};
    try {
      let customSGAddonMeta = {};
      if (customSGAddonMeta.sg_addon_custom_js) {
        Function(customSGAddonMeta.sg_addon_custom_js)();
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.warn("Error In SG Addon Custom Code", error);
    }
  })();
</script>

              </span><div class="product__unit-price product__unit-price--spacing product__unit-price-wrapper--7658435510329 hide"><span class="product__unit-price--7658435510329"></span>/<span class="product__unit-base--7658435510329"></span>

                id="ProductFormHolder-7658435510329"
                class="product-form-holder"
                data-url="/products/tresor-chaffing-dish"
                data-template="preorder"></div><div class="product-single__description rte">
                <style type="text/css"><!--td {border: 1px solid #cccccc;}br {mso-data-placement:same-cell;}--></style>
<p>Elevate your dining experience with our <strong>Handmade Silver Serving Dish</strong>. Crafted with meticulous attention to detail, this exquisite piece combines functionality with elegance. The serving bowl is made from high-quality stainless steel, ensuring durability and a luxurious look. The water compartment and stand feature a plated silver finish, adding a touch of sophistication to your table setting. The lid, crafted from brass and plated for a polished finish, completes the ensemble, making it a must-have for formal gatherings or special occasions.</p>
<h4>Dimensions:</h4>
<p><strong>Size: Small (13 inches)</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Length: 13 inches</li>
<li>Width: 10 inches</li>
<li>Height: 7 inches</li>
<li>Weight: 1.85 kg</li>
<li>Capacity: 2.2 liters</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Size: Large (18 inches)</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Length: 18 inches</li>
<li>Width: 12 inches</li>
<li>Height: 9.5 inches</li>
<li>Weight: 4.25 kg</li>
<li>Capacity: 3.15 liters</li>
</ul>
<h3>Care Instructions:</h3>
<p>Taking proper care of silver-coated serveware is essential to maintain its shine and prevent tarnishing.</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>Hand Washing:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Always wash silver-coated serveware by hand using mild dish soap and warm water.</li>
<li>Avoid using harsh chemicals or abrasive cleaners that can damage the silver coating.</li>
<li>Rinse thoroughly with clean water and dry immediately with a soft, lint-free cloth to prevent water spots.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Avoid Extended Exposure to Heat and Sunlight:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Keep silver-coated serveware away from direct sunlight and heat sources, such as stovetops or ovens, as they can cause discoloration and damage.</li>
<li>Store serveware in a cool, dry place when not in use.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Use Gentle Cleaning Methods:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Use a soft cloth or sponge to gently clean silver-coated serveware.</li>
<li>For stubborn stains or tarnish, you can use a silver polish specifically designed for silver-plated items. Follow the manufacturer's instructions carefully.</li>
<li>Avoid using abrasive materials or scrubbing vigorously, as this can scratch the silver coating.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Avoid Contact with Certain Substances:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Keep silver-coated serveware away from acidic foods, such as citrus fruits or vinegar, as they can cause tarnishing.</li>
<li>Avoid contact with salt or salty foods for extended periods, as salt can also damage the silver finish.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Regular Maintenance:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Regularly polish silver-coated serveware with a soft cloth to maintain its shine and remove any light tarnish.</li>
<li>Store serveware in a tarnish-resistant cloth or pouch to prevent tarnishing when not in use.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

                <p>Elevate your dining experience with our <strong>Handmade Silver Serving Dish</strong>. Crafted with meticulous attention to detail, this exquisite piece combines functionality with elegance. The serving bowl is made from high-quality stainless steel, ensuring durability and a luxurious look. The water compartment and stand feature a plated silver finish, adding a touch of sophistication to your table setting. The lid, crafted from brass and plated for a polished finish, completes the ensemble, making it a must-have for formal gatherings or special occasions.</p>
<h4>Dimensions:</h4>
<p><strong>Size: Small</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Length: 13 inches</li>
<li>Width: 10 inches</li>
<li>Height: 2.3 inches</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Size: Large</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Length: 18 inches</li>
<li>Width: 11.6 inches</li>
<li>Height: 2.3 inches</li>
</ul>
<h3>Care Instructions:</h3>
<p>Taking proper care of silver-coated serveware is essential to maintain its shine and prevent tarnishing.</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>Hand Washing:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Always wash silver-coated serveware by hand using mild dish soap and warm water.</li>
<li>Avoid using harsh chemicals or abrasive cleaners that can damage the silver coating.</li>
<li>Rinse thoroughly with clean water and dry immediately with a soft, lint-free cloth to prevent water spots.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Avoid Extended Exposure to Heat and Sunlight:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Keep silver-coated serveware away from direct sunlight and heat sources, such as stovetops or ovens, as they can cause discoloration and damage.</li>
<li>Store serveware in a cool, dry place when not in use.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Use Gentle Cleaning Methods:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Use a soft cloth or sponge to gently clean silver-coated serveware.</li>
<li>For stubborn stains or tarnish, you can use a silver polish specifically designed for silver-plated items. Follow the manufacturer's instructions carefully.</li>
<li>Avoid using abrasive materials or scrubbing vigorously, as this can scratch the silver coating.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Avoid Contact with Certain Substances:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Keep silver-coated serveware away from acidic foods, such as citrus fruits or vinegar, as they can cause tarnishing.</li>
<li>Avoid contact with salt or salty foods for extended periods, as salt can also damage the silver finish.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Regular Maintenance:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Regularly polish silver-coated serveware with a soft cloth to maintain its shine and remove any light tarnish.</li>
<li>Store serveware in a tarnish-resistant cloth or pouch to prevent tarnishing when not in use.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Product Information:</strong><br>Our new collection of speckled earthenware celebrates the elegance of simplicity, perfect for daily use. Each item is handcrafted by skilled artisans, ensuring every piece is unique with its own color, shape, and glaze. The speckled design adds a sophisticated touch to your dining experience. Due to the artisanal production process, slight variations in size and color are expected, contributing to the individuality of each item.</p>
<p><strong>Care Instructions:</strong><br>To ensure the longevity and beauty of your speckled earthenware collection, follow these care guidelines:</p>
<ol>
<li>
<strong>Hand Wash Only:</strong> Gently wash each piece with warm water and mild detergent. Avoid using abrasive scrubbers or harsh chemicals that could damage the glaze.</li>
<li>
<strong>Avoid Soaking:</strong> Do not soak earthenware items for extended periods as this may weaken the material and affect the glaze.</li>
<li>
<strong>Dry Thoroughly:</strong> After washing, dry each piece thoroughly with a soft cloth to prevent water spots and ensure they are completely dry before storing.</li>
</ol>

<p><strong>Product Information:</strong><br>Introducing our new collection of speckled earthenware, designed to bring the elegance of minimalism to your daily dining experience. Each piece is meticulously handmade by skilled artisans, ensuring every item is unique in color, shape, and glaze. The distinct speckled design adds sophistication and charm to your table. Due to the artisanal nature of the production process, slight variations in size and color are expected, enhancing the individuality of each item.</p>
<p><strong>Care Instructions:</strong><br>To ensure the longevity and beauty of your speckled earthenware collection, please follow these care guidelines:</p>
<ol>
<li>
<strong>Hand Wash Only:</strong> Gently wash with warm water and mild detergent. Avoid using abrasive scrubbers or harsh chemicals that could damage the glaze.</li>
<li>
<strong>Avoid Soaking:</strong> Do not soak earthenware items for extended periods, as this can weaken the material and affect the glaze.</li>
<li>
<strong>Dry Thoroughly:</strong> After washing, dry each piece thoroughly with a soft cloth to prevent water spots and ensure it is completely dry before storing.</li>
</ol>

The lid, crafted from brass and plated for a polished finish, completes the ensemble, making it a must-have for formal gatherings or special occasions.\nDimensions:\n\n\nSize: 8 inches\n\nCare Instructions:\nTo maintain the shine and quality of your silver-coated serveware, please follow these care guidelines:\n\n\nHand Washing: Always wash silver-coated serveware by hand using mild dish soap and warm water. Avoid using harsh chemicals or abrasive cleaners that could damage the silver coating. Rinse thoroughly with clean water and dry immediately with a soft, lint-free cloth to prevent water spots.\n\n\nAvoid Extended Exposure to Heat and Sunlight: Keep silver-coated serveware away from direct sunlight and heat sources, such as stovetops or ovens, as they can cause discoloration and damage. Store serveware in a cool, dry place when not in use.\n\n\nUse Gentle Cleaning Methods: Use a soft cloth or sponge to gently clean silver-coated serveware. For stubborn stains or tarnish, use a silver polish specifically designed for silver-plated items, following the manufacturer's instructions carefully. Avoid abrasive materials or vigorous scrubbing, which can scratch the silver coating.\n\n\nAvoid Contact with Certain Substances: Keep silver-coated serveware away from acidic foods like citrus fruits or vinegar, which can cause tarnishing. Avoid prolonged contact with salt or salty foods, as salt can damage the silver finish.\n\n\nRegular Maintenance: Regularly polish silver-coated serveware with a soft cloth to maintain its shine and remove any light tarnish. Store serveware in a tarnish-resistant cloth or pouch to prevent tarnishing when not in use.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n",

              </span><div class="product__unit-price product__unit-price--spacing product__unit-price-wrapper--7539193544761 hide"><span class="product__unit-price--7539193544761"></span>/<span class="product__unit-base--7539193544761"></span>
            </div><div class="product__policies rte small--text-center">
                <small><a href='/policies/shipping-policy'>Shipping</a> calculated at checkout.
</small>
              </div><hr class="hr--medium"><div
                id="ProductFormHolder-7539193544761"
                class="product-form-holder"
                data-url="/products/speckled-platter"
                data-template=""></div><div class="product-single__description rte">
                <p>Elevate your dining experience with our Handmade Silver Serving Dish. Crafted with meticulous attention to detail, this exquisite piece combines functionality with elegance. The serving bowl is made from high-quality stainless steel, ensuring durability and a luxurious look. The water compartment and stand feature a plated silver finish, adding a touch of sophistication to your table setting. The lid, crafted from brass and plated for a polished finish, completes the ensemble, making it a must-have for formal gatherings or special occasions.</p>
<p><strong>Dimensions:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>
<strong>Size:</strong> 8 inches</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Care Instructions:</strong></p>
<p>To maintain the shine and quality of your silver-coated serveware, please follow these care guidelines:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>Hand Washing:</strong> Always wash silver-coated serveware by hand using mild dish soap and warm water. Avoid using harsh chemicals or abrasive cleaners that could damage the silver coating. Rinse thoroughly with clean water and dry immediately with a soft, lint-free cloth to prevent water spots.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Avoid Extended Exposure to Heat and Sunlight:</strong> Keep silver-coated serveware away from direct sunlight and heat sources, such as stovetops or ovens, as they can cause discoloration and damage. Store serveware in a cool, dry place when not in use.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Use Gentle Cleaning Methods:</strong> Use a soft cloth or sponge to gently clean silver-coated serveware. For stubborn stains or tarnish, use a silver polish specifically designed for silver-plated items, following the manufacturer's instructions carefully. Avoid abrasive materials or vigorous scrubbing, which can scratch the silver coating.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Avoid Contact with Certain Substances:</strong> Keep silver-coated serveware away from acidic foods like citrus fruits or vinegar, which can cause tarnishing. Avoid prolonged contact with salt or salty foods, as salt can damage the silver finish.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Regular Maintenance:</strong> Regularly polish silver-coated serveware with a soft cloth to maintain its shine and remove any light tarnish. Store serveware in a tarnish-resistant cloth or pouch to prevent tarnishing when not in use.</p>
</li>
</ul>

<p>Elevate Your Dining Experience with Handmade Silver Serving Dish</p>
<p><strong>DIMENSIONS:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>Size: Small</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>
<strong>Length:</strong> 13 inches</li>
<li>
<strong>Width:</strong> 10 inches</li>
<li>
<strong>Height:</strong> 2.3 inches</li>
<li>
<strong>Weight:</strong> 1.25 kg</li>
<li>
<strong>Capacity:</strong> (Not specified)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Size: Large</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>
<strong>Length:</strong> 18 inches</li>
<li>
<strong>Width:</strong> 11.6 inches</li>
<li>
<strong>Height:</strong> 2.3 inches</li>
<li>
<strong>Weight:</strong> (Not specified)</li>
<li>
<strong>Capacity:</strong> (Not specified)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>PRODUCT INFORMATION:</strong><br>Crafted with meticulous attention to detail, this Handmade Silver Serving Dish combines functionality with elegance. The serving bowl is made from high-quality stainless steel, ensuring durability and a luxurious look. The water compartment and stand feature a plated silver finish, adding sophistication to your table setting. The lid, crafted from brass and plated for a polished finish, completes the ensemble, making it perfect for formal gatherings or special occasions.</p>
<p><strong>CARE INSTRUCTIONS:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>
<strong>Hand Washing:</strong> Always wash silver-coated serveware by hand using mild dish soap and warm water. Avoid harsh chemicals or abrasive cleaners that could damage the silver coating. Rinse thoroughly with clean water and dry immediately with a soft, lint-free cloth to prevent water spots.</li>
<li>
<strong>Avoid Extended Exposure to Heat and Sunlight:</strong> Keep silver-coated serveware away from direct sunlight and heat sources, such as stovetops or ovens, as they can cause discoloration and damage. Store serveware in a cool, dry place when not in use.</li>
<li>
<strong>Use Gentle Cleaning Methods:</strong> Use a soft cloth or sponge to gently clean silver-coated serveware. For stubborn stains or tarnish, use a silver polish specifically designed for silver-plated items, following the manufacturer's instructions carefully. Avoid abrasive materials or vigorous scrubbing, which can scratch the silver coating.</li>
<li>
<strong>Avoid Contact with Certain Substances:</strong> Keep silver-coated serveware away from acidic foods like citrus fruits or vinegar, which can cause tarnishing. Avoid prolonged contact with salt or salty foods, as salt can damage the silver finish.</li>
<li>
<strong>Regular Maintenance:</strong> Regularly polish silver-coated serveware with a soft cloth to maintain its shine and remove any light tarnish. Store serveware in a tarnish-resistant cloth or pouch to prevent tarnishing when not in use.</li>
</ul>

                Scalloped Salad Flat Platter

                id="ProductFormHolder-7541479014457"
                class="product-form-holder"
                data-url="/products/scallooped-salad-flat-platter"
                data-template=""></div><div class="product-single__description rte">
                <p>Elevate your dining experience with our Handmade Silver Serving Dish. Crafted with meticulous attention to detail, this exquisite piece combines functionality with elegance. The serving bowl is made from high-quality stainless steel, ensuring durability and a luxurious look. The water compartment and stand feature a plated silver finish, adding a touch of sophistication to your table setting. The lid, crafted from brass and plated for a polished finish, completes the ensemble, making it a must-have for formal gatherings or special occasions.</p>
<p><strong>Dimensions:</strong></p>
<p><strong>Size:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Length: 15 inches</li>
<li>Depth: 1.5 inches</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Size:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Length: 17 inches</li>
<li>Depth: 2 inches</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Care Instructions:</strong></p>
<p>Taking proper care of silver-coated serveware is essential to maintain its shine and prevent tarnishing.</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>Hand Washing:</strong><br>Always wash silver-coated serveware by hand using mild dish soap and warm water. Avoid using harsh chemicals or abrasive cleaners that can damage the silver coating. Rinse thoroughly with clean water and dry immediately with a soft, lint-free cloth to prevent water spots.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Avoid Extended Exposure to Heat and Sunlight:</strong><br>Keep silver-coated serveware away from direct sunlight and heat sources, such as stovetops or ovens, as they can cause discoloration and damage. Store serveware in a cool, dry place when not in use.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Use Gentle Cleaning Methods:</strong><br>Use a soft cloth or sponge to gently clean silver-coated serveware. For stubborn stains or tarnish, you can use a silver polish specifically designed for silver-plated items. Follow the manufacturer's instructions carefully. Avoid using abrasive materials or scrubbing vigorously, as this can scratch the silver coating.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Avoid Contact with Certain Substances:</strong><br>Keep silver-coated serveware away from acidic foods, such as citrus fruits or vinegar, as they can cause tarnishing. Avoid contact with salt or salty foods for extended periods, as salt can also damage the silver finish.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Regular Maintenance:</strong><br>Regularly polish silver-coated serveware with a soft cloth to maintain its shine and remove any light tarnish. Store serveware in a tarnish-resistant cloth or pouch to prevent tarnishing when not in use.</p>
</li>
</ul>

                <style type="text/css"><!--td {border: 1px solid #cccccc;}br {mso-data-placement:same-cell;}--></style>
<p>Elevate your dining experience with our Handmade Silver Serving Dish. Crafted with meticulous attention to detail, this exquisite piece combines functionality with elegance. The serving bowl is made from high-quality stainless steel, ensuring durability and a luxurious look. The water compartment and stand feature a plated silver finish, adding a touch of sophistication to your table setting. The lid, crafted from brass and plated for a polished finish, completes the ensemble, making it a must-have for formal gatherings or special occasions.</p>
<p><strong>Dimensions:</strong></p>
<p><strong>Size: </strong>Small (13 inches)</p>
<ul>
<li>Length: 13 inches</li>
<li>Width: 10 inches</li>
<li>Height: 7 inches</li>
<li>Weight: 1.85 kg</li>
<li>Capacity: 2.2 liters</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Size: </strong>Large (18 inches)</p>
<ul>
<li>Length: 18 inches</li>
<li>Width: 12 inches</li>
<li>Height: 9.5 inches</li>
<li>Weight: 4.25 kg</li>
<li>Capacity: 3.15 liters</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Care Instructions:</strong></p>
<p>To maintain the beauty and durability of your silver-coated serveware, please follow these care guidelines:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>Hand Washing:</strong> Always wash silver-coated serveware by hand using mild dish soap and warm water. Avoid harsh chemicals or abrasive cleaners that could damage the silver coating. Rinse thoroughly with clean water and dry immediately with a soft, lint-free cloth to prevent water spots.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Avoid Extended Exposure to Heat and Sunlight:</strong> Keep silver-coated serveware away from direct sunlight and heat sources, such as stovetops or ovens, as they can cause discoloration and damage. Store serveware in a cool, dry place when not in use.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Use Gentle Cleaning Methods:</strong> Use a soft cloth or sponge to clean silver-coated serveware gently. For stubborn stains or tarnish, use a silver polish specifically designed for silver-plated items, following the manufacturer's instructions carefully. Avoid abrasive materials or vigorous scrubbing, which can scratch the silver coating.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Avoid Contact with Certain Substances:</strong> Keep silver-coated serveware away from acidic foods like citrus fruits or vinegar, which can cause tarnishing. Avoid prolonged contact with salt or salty foods, as salt can damage the silver finish.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Regular Maintenance:</strong> Regularly polish silver-coated serveware with a soft cloth to maintain its shine and remove any light tarnish. Store serveware in a tarnish-resistant cloth or pouch to prevent tarnishing when not in use.</p>
</li>
</ul>

                <style type="text/css"><!--td {border: 1px solid #cccccc;}br {mso-data-placement:same-cell;}--></style>
<p>Elevate your dining experience with our Handmade Silver Serving Dish, expertly crafted with meticulous attention to detail. This exquisite piece combines functionality with elegance, making it an essential addition to your collection.</p>
<p><strong>Dimensions</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>Size: 13 inches (Small)</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Length: 13 inches</li>
<li>Width: 12 inches</li>
<li>Height: [Please specify]</li>
<li>Capacity: [Please specify]</li>
<li>Weight: 4.25 kg</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Size: 18 inches (Large)</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Length: 18 inches</li>
<li>Width: 12 inches</li>
<li>Height: [Please specify]</li>
<li>Capacity: [Please specify]</li>
<li>Weight: 4.25 kg</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Product Information</strong><br>This serving dish is crafted from high-quality stainless steel, ensuring durability and a luxurious appearance. The water compartment and stand feature a plated silver finish, adding sophistication to your table setting. The brass lid, plated for a polished finish, completes the ensemble, making it a must-have for formal gatherings or special occasions.</p>
<p><strong>Care Instructions</strong><br>To maintain the shine of your silver-coated serveware and prevent tarnishing, please follow these guidelines:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>Hand Washing:</strong><br>Always wash silver-coated serveware by hand using mild dish soap and warm water.<br>Avoid harsh chemicals or abrasive cleaners that can damage the silver coating.<br>Rinse thoroughly and dry immediately with a soft, lint-free cloth to prevent water spots.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Avoid Extended Exposure to Heat and Sunlight:</strong><br>Keep silver-coated serveware away from direct sunlight and heat sources to prevent discoloration and damage.<br>Store in a cool, dry place when not in use.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Use Gentle Cleaning Methods:</strong><br>Clean silver-coated serveware with a soft cloth or sponge.<br>For stubborn stains, use a silver polish designed for silver-plated items and follow the manufacturers instructions.<br>Avoid abrasive materials or vigorous scrubbing to prevent scratching.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Avoid Contact with Certain Substances:</strong><br>Keep away from acidic foods, such as citrus fruits or vinegar, as they can cause tarnishing.<br>Avoid prolonged contact with salt or salty foods, as salt can damage the silver finish.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Regular Maintenance:</strong><br>Polish silver-coated serveware regularly with a soft cloth to maintain shine and remove light tarnish.<br>Store in a tarnish-resistant cloth or pouch when not in use.</p>
</li>
</ul>

                <p>Introducing Our Speckled Earthenware Collection  Minimalist Elegance for Daily Use</p>
<p>Elevate your dining experience with our new collection of speckled earthenware, crafted with minimalist elegance in mind. Each piece is meticulously handmade by skilled artisans, ensuring a unique blend of color, shape, and glaze that enhances your table setting with sophistication.</p>
<p><strong>Dimensions:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>Small Size:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Length: 12 inches</li>
<li>Depth: 2 inches</li>
<li>Weight: 1.65 kg</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Large Size:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Length: 14 inches</li>
<li>Depth: 2 inches</li>
<li>Weight: 2.5 kg</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Product Information:</strong> Our speckled earthenware collection is designed with a subtle speckled finish, adding refined charm to everyday dining. Handmade with attention to detail, each piece is one-of-a-kind, featuring slight variations in size, color, and glaze. These differences highlight the artisanal quality, making each item a unique addition to your home.<strong></strong></p>
<p><strong>Care Instructions:</strong> To preserve the beauty and longevity of your speckled earthenware:</p>
<ol>
<li>
<strong>Hand Wash Only:</strong> Wash with warm water and mild detergent. Avoid abrasive scrubbers and harsh chemicals to protect the glaze.</li>
<li>
<strong>Avoid Soaking:</strong> Do not leave earthenware in water for extended periods, as this can weaken the material.</li>
<li>
<strong>Dry Thoroughly:</strong> Use a soft cloth to dry each piece thoroughly after washing, ensuring its completely dry before storing to prevent water spots.</li>
</ol>
